When You Grow Up
============================

|  |  |
| :--: | :-- |
| [![](../../../images/albums/60116bb7a49fb737f9536e3fe5c83af0.jpg)<br>When You Grow Up](https://emumo.xiami.com/album/433864) | **艺人**: [Priscilla Ahn](../index.md)<br>**语种**: 英语<br>**唱片公司**: Blue Note Records<br>**发行时间**: 2011年05月03日<br>**专辑类别**: 录音室专辑<br>**专辑风格**: 民谣流行 Folk Pop, 根源唱作人 Singer-Songwriter<br>**播放数**: 11084921<br>**收藏数**: 8098<br>**评论数**: 1226<br> |

## 简介

<div>
Priscilla Ahn历时三年的第二张专辑When You Grow Up终于要和大家见面，5月3号由Blue Note Records推出，先前已经推出同名单曲When You Grow Up预热。新专中与Sia, Eleni Mandell，Inara George合作。When You Grow Up是一张复古浪漫小情歌专辑，歌词上正如专辑名字一样是关于成长中生活和爱的点点滴滴，十分清新可爱。(By xiami)<br><br>
<br><br>
Priscilla Ahn’s new album, When You Grow Up, will be released by Blue Note Records on May 3rd. Featuring songwriting collaborations with Sia, Eleni Mandell and Inara George, When You Grow Up is a lovely little album full of romantic ballads and retro girl pop numbers. Lyrically, the album explores the theme of growth (hence the title) throughout the ups and downs of life and love. Musically, it’s just very, very pretty.
</div>
